\"\"\necho \"[CORE FIX] Fixing useVoice.ts - making voice recognition actually work...\"\n\ncat > \"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/common/useVoice.ts\" << 'USEVOICEEOF'\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// VISTAVIEW - useVoice Hook v3.0 (FIXED)\n// RULE-004: Voice everywhere with STT/TTS\n// RULE-008: Single mic management\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n}\n\n// RULE: Digit extraction from VV-AS-v1.0.json\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9',\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\s,.\\-]+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    } else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) {\n      digits += word;\n    }\n  }\n  // Also extract raw digits\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  const words = clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x);\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\n    return `${words.slice(0,3).join(' ')} \u2014 ${words.slice(3,6).join(' ')} \u2014 ${words.slice(6,10).join(' ')}`;\n  }\n  return words.join(' ');\n};\n\nexport const useVoice = ({ onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true }: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\n\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\n  const commandRef = useRef(onCommand);\n  const digitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\n  const retryCountRef = useRef(0);\n\n  // Keep refs updated\n  useEffect(() => { commandRef.current = onCommand; }, [onCommand]);\n  useEffect(() => { digitsRef.current = onDigits; }, [onDigits]);\n\n  // Initialize speech synthesis\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n    // Preload voices\n    const loadVoices = () => synthRef.current?.getVoices();\n    loadVoices();\n    window.speechSynthesis?.addEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\n    return () => window.speechSynthesis?.removeEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Initialize speech recognition - THIS IS THE FIX\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n\n    const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SpeechRecognition) {\n      console.warn('[useVoice] Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\n    recognition.continuous = true;\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\n\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition STARTED');\n      setIsListening(true);\n      retryCountRef.current = 0;\n    };\n\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\n\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      \n      console.log('[useVoice] Heard:', text, 'Final:', result.isFinal);\n      \n      if (text) {\n        setTranscript(text);\n      }\n\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\n        \n        // Extract and pass digits FIRST (for phone/OTP)\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\n        if (digits.length > 0) {\n          console.log('[useVoice] Extracted digits:', digits);\n          digitsRef.current?.(digits);\n        }\n        \n        // Then pass full command\n        commandRef.current?.(cmd);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'no-speech' || event.error === 'aborted') {\n        // Normal - just restart\n      } else if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        console.error('[useVoice] Microphone access denied');\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended, isActive:', isActiveRef.current);\n      if (isActiveRef.current && retryCountRef.current < 50) {\n        retryCountRef.current++;\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          try {\n            recognition.start();\n          } catch (e) {\n            console.log('[useVoice] Restart failed, retrying...');\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recRef.current = recognition;\n\n    // AUTO-START if requested\n    if (autoStart) {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Auto-starting recognition...');\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\n      // Small delay to ensure component is mounted\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        try {\n          recognition.start();\n          console.log('[useVoice] Recognition start() called');\n        } catch (e) {\n          console.log('[useVoice] Start failed, will retry');\n        }\n      }, 300);\n    }\n\n    return () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Cleanup - stopping recognition');\n      isActiveRef.current = false;\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    };\n  }, [autoStart]);\n\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] Speaking:', text);\n    setDisplayText(text);\n    \n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\n    \n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\n\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices[0];\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n\n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Done speaking');\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\n    };\n    utterance.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\n\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n  }, []);\n\n  const stop = useCallback(() => {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] startListening called');\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\n    try {\n      recRef.current?.start();\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.log('[useVoice] Already started or error');\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[useVoice] stopListening called');\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\n    try {\n      recRef.current?.stop();\n    } catch (e) {}\n    setIsListening(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsPaused(true);\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\n    try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  return {\n    isListening,\n    isSpeaking,\n    isPaused,\n    transcript,\n    displayText,\n    speak,\n    stop,\n    startListening,\n    stopListening,\n    pause,\n    resume,\n    // Export utilities for components\n    extractDigits,\n    formatPhoneNumber,\n    speakablePhone\n  };\n};\n\nexport default useVoice;\nUSEVOICEEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 useVoice.ts FIXED - Voice recognition will now actually capture speech\"\n\n# VIOLATE)\\n\\n### RULE 1: BACKUP FIRST\\n```\\nBEFORE any modification:\\n  1. Create timestamped backup\\n  2. Verify backup is readable\\n  3. Document what will change\\n  4. Only then proceed\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 2: PLAN BEFORE APPLY\\n```\\nTWO MODES:\\n  PLAN MODE:\\n    - Analyze current state\\n    - Propose changes\\n    - Show risks\\n    - Wait for approval\\n  \\n  APPLY MODE:\\n    - Execute only after approval\\n    - Log every action\\n    - Verify success\\n    - Notify completion\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 3: FIX ONLY WHAT'S BROKEN\\n```\\nDO NOT:\\n  - Delete working code\\n  - Replace entire files blindly\\n  - Remove features that work\\n\\nDO:\\n  - Identify specific broken function\\n  - Fix only that function\\n  - Preserve everything else\\n  - Test after fix\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 4: VOICE EVERYWHERE\\n```\\nALL user interactions must have:\\n  - Speech-to-Text (STT) input option\\n  - Text-to-Speech (TTS) feedback\\n  - Visual transcript display\\n  - Fallback to text input\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 5: CONTINUOUS NARRATION\\n```\\nDuring processing:\\n  - Speak each step as it starts\\n  - Show progress visually\\n  - Allow background browsing\\n  - Notify on completion\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 6: SPLIT LARGE OPERATIONS\\n```\\nWhen creating scripts:\\n  - If > 500 lines, split into parts\\n  - Each part is self-contained\\n  - Parts can run independently\\n  - Clear naming: PART_1, PART_2, etc.\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 7: DATA PERSISTENCE\\n```\\nAll user data must be:\\n  - Saved to database (ai-data.json)\\n  - Vectorized for AI learning\\n  - Timestamped (created, updated)\\n  - Recoverable from backup\\n```\\n\\n### RULE 8: SINGLE MIC RULE\\n```\\nOnly ONE voice interface at a time:\\n  - Landing page OR modal OR dashboard\\n  - When modal opens \\u2192 pause main mic\\n  - When modal closes \\u2192 resume main mic\\n  - Never two mics simultaneously\\n```\\n\\n## \\ud83d\\udd27 OPERATIONAL PARAMETERS\\n\\n### 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\\n  'five': '5',\\n  'six': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9',\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\\\s,.\\\\-]+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    } else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) {\\n      digits += word;\\n    }\\n  }\\n  // Also extract raw digits\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const w: Record<string, string> = {\\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\\n  };\\n  const clean = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  const words = clean.split('').map(x => w[x] || x);\\n  if (clean.length >= 10) {\\n    return `${words.slice(0,3).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${words.slice(3,6).join(' ')} \\u2014 ${words.slice(6,10).join(' ')}`;\\n  }\\n  return words.join(' ');\\n};\\n\\nexport const useVoice = ({ onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true }: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\\n\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\\n  const commandRef = useRef(onCommand);\\n  const digitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\\n  const retryCountRef = useRef(0);\\n\\n  // Keep refs updated\\n  useEffect(() => { commandRef.current = onCommand; }, [onCommand]);\\n  useEffect(() => { digitsRef.current = onDigits; }, [onDigits]);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech synthesis\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    // Preload voices\\n    const loadVoices = () => synthRef.current?.getVoices();\\n    loadVoices();\\n    window.speechSynthesis?.addEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\\n    return () => window.speechSynthesis?.removeEventListener('voiceschanged', loadVoices);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech recognition - THIS IS THE FIX\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n\\n    const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SpeechRecognition) {\\n      console.warn('[useVoice] Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\\n    recognition.continuous = true;\\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\\n\\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition STARTED');\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n      retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\\n\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      \\n      console.log('[useVoice] Heard:', text, 'Final:', result.isFinal);\\n      \\n      if (text) {\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n      }\\n\\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\\n        \\n        // Extract and pass digits FIRST (for phone/OTP)\\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n        if (digits.length > 0) {\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Extracted digits:', digits);\\n          digitsRef.current?.(digits);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Then pass full command\\n        commandRef.current?.(cmd);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'no-speech' || event.error === 'aborted') {\\n        // Normal - just restart\\n      } else if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        console.error('[useVoice] Microphone access denied');\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Recognition ended, isActive:', isActiveRef.current);\\n      if (isActiveRef.current && retryCountRef.current < 50) {\\n        retryCountRef.current++;\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          try {\\n            recognition.start();\\n          } catch (e) {\\n            console.log('[useVoice] Restart failed, retrying...');\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    recRef.current = recognition;\\n\\n    // AUTO-START if requested\\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Auto-starting recognition...');\\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\\n      // Small delay to ensure component is mounted\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        try {\\n          recognition.start();\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Recognition start() called');\\n        } catch (e) {\\n          console.log('[useVoice] Start failed, will retry');\\n        }\\n      }, 300);\\n    }\\n\\n    return () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Cleanup - stopping recognition');\\n      isActiveRef.current = false;\\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n    };\\n  }, [autoStart]);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] Speaking:', text);\\n    setDisplayText(text);\\n    \\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n\\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices[0];\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n\\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Done speaking');\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    };\\n    utterance.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\\n\\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stop = useCallback(() => {\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] startListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.start();\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.log('[useVoice] Already started or error');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[useVoice] stopListening called');\\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\\n    try {\\n      recRef.current?.stop();\\n    } catch (e) {}\\n    setIsListening(false);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\\n    setIsPaused(true);\\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    retryCountRef.current = 0;\\n    try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch (e) {}\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  return {\\n    isListening,\\n    isSpeaking,\\n    isPaused,\\n    transcript,\\n    displayText,\\n    speak,\\n    stop,\\n    startListening,\\n    stopListening,\\n    pause,\\n    resume,\\n    // Export utilities for components\\n    extractDigits,\\n    formatPhoneNumber,\\n    speakablePhone\\n  };\\n};\\n\\nexport default useVoice;\\nUSEVOICEEOF\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 useVoice.ts FIXED - Voice recognition will now actually capture speech\\\"\\n\\n# fill boxes and auto-tab\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Received voice digits:', digits);\n    \n    const cleanDigits = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (cleanDigits.length === 0) return;\n    \n    setError('');\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\n    \n    // Find first empty slot\n    let startIdx = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\n    if (startIdx === -1) startIdx = 0; // If all filled, start from beginning\n    \n    // Fill in digits\n    for (let i = 0; i < cleanDigits.length && startIdx + i < 6; i++) {\n      newOtp[startIdx + i] = cleanDigits[i];\n    }\n    \n    setOtp(newOtp);\n    speak(cleanDigits.split('').join(' '));\n    \n    // Focus next empty or last\n    const nextEmpty = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\n    if (nextEmpty !== -1) {\n      inputRefs.current[nextEmpty]?.focus();\n    } else {\n      inputRefs.current[5]?.focus();\n      // Auto-verify when complete\n      setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(newOtp.join('')), 500);\n    }\n  }, [otp, speak]);\n\n  // Register handler\n  useEffect(() => {\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Registering voice digit handler');\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\n\n  // Handle typed input with AUTO-TAB\n  const handleChange = (index: number, value: string) => {\n    const digit = value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(-1);\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\n    newOtp[index] = digit;\n    setOtp(newOtp);\n    setError('');\n\n    // AUTO-TAB to next input\n    if (digit && index < 5) {\n      inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\n    }\n\n    // Auto-verify when all filled\n    if (digit && newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\n      setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(newOtp.join('')), 300);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Handle backspace - go to previous\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\n    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) {\n      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Handle paste\n  const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    const pasted = e.clipboardData.getData('text').replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6);\n    if (pasted.length > 0) {\n      const newOtp = [...otp];\n      for (let i = 0; i < pasted.length; i++) {\n        newOtp[i] = pasted[i];\n      }\n      setOtp(newOtp);\n      if (pasted.length === 6) {\n        setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(pasted), 300);\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Verify OTP\n  const verifyOTP = (code: string) => {\n    if (verifying || verified) return;\n    \n    setVerifying(true);\n    speak(\"Verifying code...\");\n    \n    setTimeout(() => {\n      if (code === DEMO_OTP) {\n        setVerified(true);\n        speak(\"Code verified! Welcome aboard!\");\n        setTimeout(onVerified, 1500);\n      } else {\n        setError('Incorrect code. Use 123456 for demo.');\n        speak(\"That code is incorrect. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        setVerifying(false);\n        // Clear and focus first\n        setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n        inputRefs.current[0]?.focus();\n      }\n    }, 1000);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n        Enter Verification Code\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '8px', fontSize: '0.95em' }}>\n        Sent to <strong style={{ color: '#fff' }}>{phone}</strong>\n      </p>\n      <p style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\n        Demo code: <strong style={{ color: THEME.goldLight }}>1 2 3 4 5 6</strong>\n      </p>\n\n      {/* OTP Input Boxes */}\n      <div style={{ \n        display: 'flex', \n        justifyContent: 'center', \n        gap: '10px', \n        marginBottom: '20px' \n      }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, index) => (\n          <input\n            key={index}\n            ref={(el) => { inputRefs.current[index] = el; }}\n            type=\"text\"\n            inputMode=\"numeric\"\n            maxLength={1}\n            value={digit}\n            onChange={(e) => handleChange(index, e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(index, e)}\n            onPaste={index === 0 ? handlePaste : undefined}\n            disabled={verifying || verified}\n            autoFocus={index === 0}\n            style={{\n              width: '50px',\n              height: '60px',\n              fontSize: '1.8em',\n              textAlign: 'center',\n              borderRadius: '12px',\n              border: `2px solid ${error ? '#e74c3c' : digit ? '#4CAF50' : THEME.gold}`,\n              background: digit ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.1)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontWeight: 600,\n              outline: 'none',\n              transition: 'all 0.2s'\n            }}\n          />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Error */}\n      {error && (\n        <p style={{ color: '#e74c3c', fontSize: '0.9em', marginBottom: '16px' }}>\n          \u26a0\ufe0f {error}\n        </p>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Status */}\n      {verifying && !verified && (\n        <div style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '16px' }}>\n          \u23f3 Verifying...\n        </div>\n      )}\n      {verified && (\n        <div style={{ color: '#4CAF50', marginBottom: '16px', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>\n          \u2713 Verified! Continuing...\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Resend */}\n      {!verified && !verifying && (\n        <button\n          onClick={() => speak(\"A new code has been sent.\")}\n          style={{\n            background: 'transparent',\n            border: 'none',\n            color: THEME.gold,\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            textDecoration: 'underline',\n fill boxes and auto-tab\\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Received voice digits:', digits);\\n    \\n    const cleanDigits = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (cleanDigits.length === 0) return;\\n    \\n    setError('');\\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\\n    \\n    // Find first empty slot\\n    let startIdx = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\\n    if (startIdx === -1) startIdx = 0; // If all filled, start from beginning\\n    \\n    // Fill in digits\\n    for (let i = 0; i < cleanDigits.length && startIdx + i < 6; i++) {\\n      newOtp[startIdx + i] = cleanDigits[i];\\n    }\\n    \\n    setOtp(newOtp);\\n    speak(cleanDigits.split('').join(' '));\\n    \\n    // Focus next empty or last\\n    const nextEmpty = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\\n    if (nextEmpty !== -1) {\\n      inputRefs.current[nextEmpty]?.focus();\\n    } else {\\n      inputRefs.current[5]?.focus();\\n      // Auto-verify when complete\\n      setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(newOtp.join('')), 500);\\n    }\\n  }, [otp, speak]);\\n\\n  // Register handler\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Registering voice digit handler');\\n    onVoiceDigits?.(handleVoiceDigits);\\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\\n\\n  // Handle typed input with AUTO-TAB\\n  const handleChange = (index: number, value: string) => {\\n    const digit = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(-1);\\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\\n    newOtp[index] = digit;\\n    setOtp(newOtp);\\n    setError('');\\n\\n    // AUTO-TAB to next input\\n    if (digit && index < 5) {\\n      inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\\n    }\\n\\n    // Auto-verify when all filled\\n    if (digit && newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\\n      setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(newOtp.join('')), 300);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle backspace - go to previous\\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\\n    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) {\\n      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle paste\\n  const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    const pasted = e.clipboardData.getData('text').replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6);\\n    if (pasted.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = [...otp];\\n      for (let i = 0; i < pasted.length; i++) {\\n        newOtp[i] = pasted[i];\\n      }\\n      setOtp(newOtp);\\n      if (pasted.length === 6) {\\n        setTimeout(() => verifyOTP(pasted), 300);\\n      }\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Verify OTP\\n  const verifyOTP = (code: string) => {\\n    if (verifying || verified) return;\\n    \\n    setVerifying(true);\\n    speak(\\\"Verifying code...\\\");\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      if (code === DEMO_OTP) {\\n        setVerified(true);\\n        speak(\\\"Code verified! Welcome aboard!\\\");\\n        setTimeout(onVerified, 1500);\\n      } else {\\n        setError('Incorrect code. Use 123456 for demo.');\\n        speak(\\\"That code is incorrect. \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport React, { useState, useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport AgentBar from '../common/AgentBar';\nimport { useVoice, extractDigits, formatPhoneNumber, speakablePhone } from '../common/useVoice';\nimport { useNavStack } from '../common/useNavStack';\nimport VendorPhone from './VendorPhone';\nimport VendorOTP from './VendorOTP';\nimport VendorProfile from './VendorProfile';\nimport VendorDashboard from './VendorDashboard';\nimport VendorUpload from './VendorUpload';\nimport VendorPipeline from './VendorPipeline';\n\ninterface VendorFlowProps {\n  isOpen: boolean;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onComplete: () => void;\n  onBack: () => void;\n}\n\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'dashboard' | 'upload' | 'pipeline' | 'complete';\n\nconst STEPS: { id: Step; label: string }[] = [\n  { id: 'phone', label: 'Phone' },\n  { id: 'otp', label: 'Verify' },\n  { id: 'profile', label: 'Profile' },\n  { id: 'dashboard', label: 'Dashboard' },\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\n];\n\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\n    phone: '',\n    vendorId: '',\n    profile: '',\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\n    companyName: '',\n    catalogFile: null as File | null,\n    products: [] as any[]\n  });\n\n  // CRITICAL: Refs to pass voice digits to child components\n  const voiceDigitHandlerRef = useRef<((digits: string) => void) | null>(null);\n\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone' });\n\n  // Voice command handler\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd);\n    \n    // Global commands\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\n      voice.stop();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || cmd.includes('cancel')) {\n      voice.stop();\n      onClose();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\n      goBack();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Phone\n    if (step === 'phone') {\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\n          goToStep('otp');\n          voice.speak(\"Sending code. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Profile\n    if (step === 'profile') {\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('next')) {\n        saveProfile();\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('beautify') || cmd.includes('enhance')) {\n        voice.speak(\"Enhancing your profile with AI...\");\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Dashboard\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\n        goToStep('upload');\n        voice.speak(\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\");\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Step-specific: Complete\n    if (step === 'complete') {\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\n        onComplete();\n      }\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\n        onClose();\n      }\n    }\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\n\n  // CRITICAL: Voice digit handler - passes to child components\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Received digits:', digits, 'Current step:', step);\n    // Pass to the registered handler (VendorPhone or VendorOTP)\n    if (voiceDigitHandlerRef.current) {\n      voiceDigitHandlerRef.current(digits);\n    }\n  }, [step]);\n\n  const voice = useVoice({ \n    onCommand: handleCommand, \n    onDigits: handleDigits,\n    autoStart: isOpen \n  });\n\n  // Navigation\n  const goBack = () => {\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx <= 0) {\n      onBack();\n    } else {\n      const prev = order[idx - 1];\n      setStep(prev);\n      navStack.pop();\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\n    setStep(newStep);\n  };\n\n  // Save profile to backend\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\n    voice.speak(\"Saving your profile...\");\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say 'upload catalog' to add products.\");\n    } catch (e) {\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\n      goToStep('dashboard');\n      voice.speak(\"Profile saved locally. Say 'upload catalog' to continue.\");\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Welcome on open\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        voice.speak(\"Welcome, Vendor! Let's set you up. Tell me your phone number. Say each digit clearly.\");\n      }, 500);\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  // Cleanup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!isOpen) {\n      voice.stop();\n      voice.stopListening();\n      setStep('phone');\n    }\n  }, [isOpen]);\n\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ \n      position: 'fixed', inset: 0, \n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', \n      zIndex: 10000, \n      display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', \n      padding: '20px' \n    }}>\n      <div style={{ \n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, \n        borderRadius: '20px', \n        width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', \n        overflow: 'hidden', \n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`,\n        display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column'\n      }}>\n        \n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{ \n          padding: '16px 24px', \n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, \n          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' \n        }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83d\udce6</span>\n            <div>\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{\n            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff',\n            width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em'\n          }}>\u2715</button>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: '4px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ \n              flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', \n              background: stepIndex >= i ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)'\n            }} />\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Agent Bar */}\n        <AgentBar\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\n          onStop={voice.stop}\n          onPause={voice.pause}\n          onResume={voice.resume}\n          onBack={goBack}\n          onClose={onClose}\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\n          showModes={true}\n          showNavButtons={true}\n        />\n\n        {/* Content */}\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\n          \n          {step === 'phone' && (\n            <VendorPhone\n              value={vendorData.phone}\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\n              onNext={() => {\n                goToStep('otp');\n                voice.speak(`Sending code to ${speakablePhone(vendorData.phone)}. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.`);\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'otp' && (\n            <VendorOTP\n              phone={formatPhoneNumber(vendorData.phone)}\n              onVerified={() => {\n                goToStep('profile');\n                voice.speak(\"Verified! Now tell me about your business.\");\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'profile' && (\n            <VendorProfile\n              profile={vendorData.profile}\n              beautified={vendorData.beautifiedProfile}\n              companyName={vendorData.companyName}\n              onChange={(profile) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, profile }))}\n              onCompanyChange={(name) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, companyName: name }))}\n              onBeautify={(b) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, beautifiedProfile: b }))}\n              onSave={saveProfile}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'dashboard' && (\n            <VendorDashboard\n              vendorName={vendorData.companyName || 'Your Store'}\n              onUploadCatalog={() => {\n                goToStep('upload');\n                voice.speak(\"Upload your catalog. I'll process it and publish your products.\");\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'upload' && (\n            <VendorUpload\n              onFileSelected={(file) => {\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, catalogFile: file }));\n                goToStep('pipeline');\n                voice.speak(`Processing ${file.name}. You can browse the homepage while I work. I'll notify you when done.`);\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\n            <VendorPipeline\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\n              vendorId={vendorData.vendorId}\n              onComplete={(products) => {\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\n                setStep('complete');\n                voice.speak(\"Congratulations! Your catalog is live on VistaView!\");\n              }}\n              speak={voice.speak}\n              onBrowseHome={() => {\n                voice.speak(\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing and notify you when done.\");\n                // Could minimize modal here\n              }}\n            />\n          )}\n\n          {step === 'complete' && (\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\n              <div style={{ \n                width: '100px', height: '100px', borderRadius: '50%', \n                background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #4CAF50, #2E7D32)', \n                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',\n                margin: '0 auto 24px', boxShadow: '0 0 30px rgba(76,175,80,0.4)'\n              }}>\n                <span style={{ fontSize: '3em', color: '#fff' }}>\u2713</span>\n              </div>\n              \n              <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginBottom: '12px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\n                \ud83c\udf89 You're Live on VistaView!\n              </h3>\n              <p style={{ color: '#aaa', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n                {vendorData.products?.length || 0} products published\n              </p>\n              <p style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: '32px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\n                Find your store in Product Catalogue\n              </p>\n              \n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>\n                <button onClick={onComplete} style={{ \n                  padding: '14px 32px', background: THEME.gold, color: '#000', \n                  border: 'none', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 600\n                }}>\n                  \ud83d\udce6 View My Products\n                </button>\n                <button onClick={() => setStep('dashboard')} style={{ \n                  padding: '14px 24px', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', color: '#fff', \n                  border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}`, borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer'\n                }}>\n                  \u2190 Dashboard\n                </button>\n                <button onClick={onClose} style={{ \n                  padding: '14px 24px', background: 'transparent', color: '#888', \n                  border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2)', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer'\n                }}>\n                  Done\n                </button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport '../common/useVoice';\\nimport { useNavStack } from '../common/useNavStack';\\nimport VendorPhone from './VendorPhone';\\nimport VendorOTP from './VendorOTP';\\nimport VendorProfile from label: 'Dashboard' },\\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\\n];\\n\\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\\n    phone: '',\\n    vendorId: '',\\n    profile: '',\\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\\n    companyName: '',\\n    catalogFile: null as File | null,\\n    products: [] as any[]\\n  });\\n\\n  // CRITICAL: Refs to pass voice digits to child components\\n  const voiceDigitHandlerRef = useRef<((digits: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n\\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone' });\\n\\n  // Voice command handler\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Command:', cmd);\\n    \\n    // Global commands\\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || cmd.includes('cancel')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      onClose();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\\n      goBack();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Phone\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('correct') || cmd.includes('confirm')) {\\n        if (vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\n          goToStep('otp');\\n          voice.speak(\\\"Sending code. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\");\\n        }\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Profile\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('next')) {\\n        saveProfile();\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('beautify') || cmd.includes('enhance')) {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Enhancing your profile with AI...\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Dashboard\\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\\n        goToStep('upload');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. I accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific: Complete\\n    if (step === 'complete') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog')) {\\n        onComplete();\\n      }\\n      if (cmd.includes('done') || cmd.includes('finish')) {\\n        onClose();\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // CRITICAL: Voice digit handler - passes to child components\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorFlow] Received digits:', digits, 'Current step:', step);\\n    // Pass to the registered handler (VendorPhone or VendorOTP)\\n    if (voiceDigitHandlerRef.current) {\\n      voiceDigitHandlerRef.current(digits);\\n    }\\n  }, [step]);\\n\\n  const voice = useVoice({ \\n    onCommand: handleCommand, \\n    onDigits: handleDigits,\\n    autoStart: isOpen \\n  });\\n\\n  // Navigation\\n  const goBack = () => {\\n    const order: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\\n    const idx = order.indexOf(step);\\n    if (idx <= 0) {\\n      onBack();\\n    } else {\\n      const prev = order[idx - 1];\\n      setStep(prev);\\n      navStack.pop();\\n      voice.speak(`Going back to ${STEPS.find(s => s.id === prev)?.label}.`);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const goToStep = (newStep: Step) => {\\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label: STEPS.find(s => s.id === newStep)?.label || newStep });\\n    setStep(newStep);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Save profile to backend\\n  const saveProfile = async () => {\\n    voice.speak(\\\"Saving your profile...\\\");\\n    try {\\n      const res = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/vendors', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({\\n          phone: vendorData.phone,\\n          profile: vendorData.beautifiedProfile || vendorData.profile,\\n          companyName: vendorData.companyName,\\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()\\n        })\\n      });\\n      const data = await res.json();\\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, vendorId: data.id }));\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard. Say 'upload catalog' to add products.\\\");\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      console.error('Save failed:', e);\\n      goToStep('dashboard');\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved locally. Say 'upload catalog' to continue.\\\");\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Welcome on open\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone') {\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Welcome, Vendor! Let's set you up. Tell me your phone number. Say each digit clearly.\\\");\\n      }, 500);\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  // Cleanup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!isOpen) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      voice.stopListening();\\n      setStep('phone');\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\\n\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\\n  const canGoBack = step !== 'phone';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ \\n      position: 'fixed', inset: 0, \\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', \\n      zIndex: 10000, \\n      display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', \\n      padding: '20px' \\n    }}>\\n      <div style={{ \\n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, \\n        borderRadius: '20px', \\n        width: '100%', maxWidth: '850px', maxHeight: '92vh', \\n        overflow: 'hidden', \\n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`,\\n        display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column'\\n      }}>\\n        \\n        {/* Header */}\\n        <div style={{ \\n          padding: '16px 24px', \\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, \\n          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' \\n        }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\\ud83d\\udce6</span>\\n            <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\\n            </div>\\n          </div>\\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{\\n            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff',\\n            width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em'\\n          }}>\\u2715</button>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Progress Bar */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: '4px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ \\n              flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', \\n              background: stepIndex >= i ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)'\\n            }} />\\n          ))}\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Agent Bar */}\\n        <AgentBar\\n          isListening={voice.isListening}\\n          isSpeaking={voice.isSpeaking}\\n          isPaused={voice.isPaused}\\n          transcript={voice.transcript}\\n          displayText={voice.displayText}\\n          onStop={voice.stop}\\n          onPause={voice.pause}\\n          onResume={voice.resume}\\n          onBack={goBack}\\n          onClose={onClose}\\n          canGoBack={canGoBack}\\n          showModes={true}\\n          showNavButtons={true}\\n        />\\n\\n        {/* Content */}\\n        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', padding: '24px' }}>\\n          \\n          {step === 'phone' && (\\n            <VendorPhone\\n              value={vendorData.phone}\\n              onChange={(phone) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }))}\\n              onNext={() => {\\n                goToStep('otp');\\n                voice.speak(`Sending code to ${speakablePhone(vendorData.phone)}. Enter 1 2 3 4 5 6 for demo.`);\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'otp' && (\\n            <VendorOTP\\n              phone={formatPhoneNumber(vendorData.phone)}\\n              onVerified={() => {\\n                goToStep('profile');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Verified! Now tell me about your business.\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onVoiceDigits={(handler) => { voiceDigitHandlerRef.current = handler; }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'profile' && (\\n            <VendorProfile\\n              profile={vendorData.profile}\\n              beautified={vendorData.beautifiedProfile}\\n              companyName={vendorData.companyName}\\n              onChange={(profile) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, profile }))}\\n              onCompanyChange={(name) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, companyName: name }))}\\n              onBeautify={(b) => setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, beautifiedProfile: b }))}\\n              onSave={saveProfile}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'dashboard' && (\\n            <VendorDashboard\\n              vendorName={vendorData.companyName || 'Your Store'}\\n              onUploadCatalog={() => {\\n                goToStep('upload');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. I'll process it and publish your products.\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'upload' && (\\n            <VendorUpload\\n              onFileSelected={(file) => {\\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, catalogFile: file }));\\n                goToStep('pipeline');\\n                voice.speak(`Processing ${file.name}. You can browse the homepage while I work. I'll notify you when done.`);\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'pipeline' && (\\n            <VendorPipeline\\n              fileName={vendorData.catalogFile?.name}\\n              vendorId={vendorData.vendorId}\\n              onComplete={(products) => {\\n                setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, products }));\\n                setStep('complete');\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Congratulations! Your catalog is live on VistaView!\\\");\\n              }}\\n              speak={voice.speak}\\n              onBrowseHome={() => {\\n                voice.speak(\\\"Feel free to browse. I'll keep processing and notify you when done.\\\");\\n                // Could minimize modal here\\n              }}\\n            />\\n          )}\\n\\n          {step === 'complete' && (\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '40px 20px' }}>\\n              <div style={{ \\n                width: '100px', height: '100px', borderRadius: '50%', \\n                background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #4CAF50, #2E7D32)', \\n                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',\\n                margin: '0 auto 24px', boxShadow: '0 0 30px THEME.gold, marginBottom: '12px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n                \\ud83c\\udf89 You're Live on VistaView!\\n              </h3>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#aaa', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\\n                {vendorData.products?.length || 0} products published\\n              </p>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: '32px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n                Find your store in Product Catalogue\\n              </p>\\n              \\n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>\\n                <button onClick={onComplete} style={{ \\n                  padding: '14px 32px', background: THEME.gold, color: '#000', \\n                  border: 'none', borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer',           padding: '14px 24px', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', color: '#fff', \\n                  border: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}`, borderRadius: '25px', cursor: 'pointer'\\n I'll narrate each step.\");\n    let i = 0;\n    const run = () => {\n      if (!mounted.current) return;\n      if (i < STEPS.length) {\n        setStep(i + 1);\n        speak(STEPS[i].say);\n        const start = (i / STEPS.length) * 100, end = ((i + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100, t0 = Date.now();\n        const animate = () => {\n          if (!mounted.current) return;\n          const p = Math.min((Date.now() - t0) / STEPS[i].duration, 1);\n          setProgress(start + (end - start) * p);\n          if (p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n          else { i++; setTimeout(run, 800); }\n        };\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n      } else {\n        speak(\"Done! Your products are live.\");\n        setTimeout(() => mounted.current && onComplete([{ id: '1', name: 'Sample Product', price: 99 }]), 1500);\n      }\n    };\n    setTimeout(run, 1000);\n    return () => { mounted.current = false; };\n  }, []);\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\u2699\ufe0f</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px' }}>Processing</h3>\n      {fileName && <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>{fileName}</p>}\n      <div style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderRadius: '10px', height: '20px', margin: '20px 0', overflow: 'hidden' }}>\n        <div style={{ background: THEME.gold, height: '100%', width: `${progress}%`, transition: 'width 0.1s' }} />\n      </div>\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'left', maxWidth: '400px', margin: '0 auto' }}>\n        {STEPS.map((s, idx) => (\n          <div key={idx} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', padding: '8px', background: step === idx + 1 ? 'rgba(184,134,11,0.15)' : 'transparent', borderRadius: '8px', marginBottom: '4px' }}>\n            <span style={{ width: '28px', height: '28px', borderRadius: '50%', background: step > idx + 1 ? '#4CAF50' : step === idx + 1 ? THEME.gold : '#333', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>{step > idx + 1 ? '\u2713' : s.icon}</span>\n            <span style={{ color: step > idx + 1 ? '#4CAF50' : step === idx + 1 ? '#fff' : '#666' }}>{s.label}</span>\n          </div>\n        ))}\n      </div>\n      {step >= 2 && onBrowseHome && <button onClick={onBrowseHome} style={{ marginTop: '20px', padding: '10px 20px', background: 'transparent', border: '1px solid #555', color: '#888', borderRadius: '20px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>\ud83c\udfe0 Browse while processing</button>}\n    </div>\n  );\n};\nexport default VendorPipeline;\nEOF\necho \"  \u2705 VendorPipeline.tsx\"\n\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# VendorProfile.tsx - LinkedIn-style\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\necho \"[4/6] Creating VendorProfile.tsx...\"\ncat > \"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorProfile.tsx\" << 'EOF'\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\ninterface Props { profile: string; I'll narrate each step.\\\");\\n    let i = 0;\\n    const run = () => {\\n      if (!mounted.current) return;\\n      if (i < STEPS.length) {\\n        setStep(i + 1);\\n        speak(STEPS[i].say);\\n        const start = (i / STEPS.length) * 100, end = ((i + 1) / STEPS.length) * 100, t0 = Date.now();\\n        const animate = () => {\\n          if (!mounted.current) return;\\n          const p = Math.min((Date.now() - t0) / STEPS[i].duration, 1);\\n          setProgress(start + (end - start) * p);\\n          if (p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n          else { i++; setTimeout(run, 800); }\\n        };\\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n      } else {\\n        speak(\\\"Done! Your products are live.\\\");\\n        setTimeout(() => mounted.current && onComplete([{ id: '1', name: 'Sample Product', price: 99 }]), 1500);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    setTimeout(run, 1000);\\n    return () => { mounted.current = false; };\\n  }, []);\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\u2699\\ufe0f</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px' }}>Processing</h3>\\n      {fileName && <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>{fileName}</p>}\\n      <div style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderRadius: '10px', height: '20px', margin: '20px 0', overflow: 'hidden' }}>\\n        <div style={{ background: THEME.gold, height: '100%', width: `${progress}%`, transition: 'width 0.1s' }} />\\n      </div>\\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'left', maxWidth: '400px', margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n        {STEPS.map((s, idx) => (\\n          <div key={idx} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', padding: '8px', background: step === idx + 1 ? 'rgba(184,134,11,0.15)' : 'transparent', borderRadius: '8px', marginBottom: '4px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ width: '28px', height: '28px', borderRadius: '50%', background: step > idx + 1 ? '#4CAF50' : step === idx + 1 ? THEME.gold : '#333', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>{step > idx + 1 ? '\\u2713' : s.icon}</span>\\n            <span style={{ color: step > idx + 1 ? '#4CAF50' : step === idx + 1 ? '#fff' : '#666' }}>{s.label}</span>\\n          </div>\\n        ))}\\n      </div>\\n      {step >= 2 && onBrowseHome && <button onClick={onBrowseHome} style={{ marginTop: '20px', padding: '10px 20px', background: 'transparent', border: '1px solid #555', color: '#888', borderRadius: '20px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>\\ud83c\\udfe0 Browse while processing</button>}\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\nexport default VendorPipeline;\\nEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 VendorPipeline.tsx\\\"\\n\\n# \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# VendorProfile.tsx - LinkedIn-style\\n# \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"[4/6] Creating VendorProfile.tsx...\\\"\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorProfile.tsx\\\" << 'EOF'\\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\ninterface Props { profile: string;
